country_event = { #The Situation of the French Republic - History
	id = nfa.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.1"}
	title = nfa.1.t
	desc = nfa.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_NFA_Early1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.1.a #Political Situation
		NFA = {
			country_event = {
				id = nfa.2
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Lion in Canada
	id = nfa.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.5"}
	title = nfa.5.t
	desc = nfa.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CAN_edward2

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.5.a #Time to return home
		NFA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = committed_to_return_home
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = committed_to_return_home
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NFA = {
				country_event = {
					id = nfa.6 days = 14
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Setup
	id = nfa.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.6"}
	title = nfa.6.t
	desc = nfa.6.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.6.a #Let's see what they wrote
		hidden_effect = {
			NFA = {
				country_event = {
					id = nfa.7 days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { #Set up the variables for the power struggle
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_influence
				value = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Mor_influence
				value = 2
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Pet_corruption
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = Competition_Loop_Counter
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Book Competition - Books
	id = nfa.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.7"}
	title = nfa.7.t
	desc = nfa.7.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.7.a #Support Mordacq
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_AF
					}
					has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_RF
                    }
                }
            }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = nfa.8 days = 10
			}
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.7.b #Support CdG
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_SUS
                    }
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_CSN
                    }
                }
            }
		}
		hidden_effect = {

				id = nfa.9 days = 10
			}
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.7.c #Let it run it's course

			factor = 30
			modifier = {
                factor = 0

                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_CSN

                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_AF
					}
					has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_RF

            }

country_event = { #Franchet d'Espèrey Retires
	id = nfa.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.13"}
	title = nfa.13.t
	desc = nfa.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_TheOtherMarshal

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.13.a #Pass the Torch to the Bear
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_AF
					}
					has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_RF
                    }
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
						option = NFA_START_EMPIRE_ABSOLUTISM
					}
                }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 804
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 806 } #Mordacq
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.16 days = 15 }
			set_country_flag = Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_dead
			remove_ideas = NFA_Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_cos_pau
			remove_ideas = NFA_Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_hog_pau
		}
		add_ideas = NFA_Henri_Mordacq_hog_ade
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.13.b #Lion Undivided
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 38
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_SUS
                    }
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_CSN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_AF
					}
					has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_RF
                    }
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
						option = NFA_START_EMPIRE_ABSOLUTISM
					}
                }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0 }
			set_country_flag = Petain_headstart_cf #Gives Petain a slight boost in the Fight for Influence
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 804
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.19 days = 15 }
			set_country_flag = Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_dead
			remove_ideas = NFA_Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_cos_pau
			remove_ideas = NFA_Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_hog_pau
		}
		add_ideas = NFA_Philippe_Petain_hog_pau
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.13.c #Young Guard
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 32
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_SUS
                    }
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_CSN
                    }
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
						option = NFA_START_EMPIRE_ABSOLUTISM
					}
                }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			add_political_power = -50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			}
			clr_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen_0
			set_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 804
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 802 } #CdG
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = nfa.43 days = 10 }
			set_country_flag = Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_dead
			remove_ideas = NFA_Louis_Franchet_d'Esperey_cos_pau
		}
		add_ideas = NFA_Charles_de_Gaulle_hog_npo
	}
	option = {
		name = nfa.13.e #Napoléon Gang
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
                factor = 0
                OR = {
                    has_game_rule = {
                        rule = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH
                        option = NFA_GOVERNMENT_PATH_SUS

                    }

		}
		if = {

			}

country_event = { #Put Mordacq in charge
	id = nfa.17
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.17"}

	desc = nfa.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_NFA_event_NFA_Mordacq

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.17.a #Général, bienvenue!
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = { 
				name = "Henri Mordacq"
				desc = "POLITICS_HENRI_MORDACQ_ELECT_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_NFA_Henri_Mordacq.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				traits = {
					NFA_Bear_Elect
				}
			}
		}
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			NFA_Francois_de_la_Rocque_hog_ade
			NFA_Camille_Barrere_for_sco
			NFA_Marie_Eugene_Debeney_eco_ade
			NFA_Ernest_Mercier_sec_pau
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			NFA = {
				country_event = {
					id = nfa.89 days = 25
				}
				country_event = {
					id = nfa.91 days = 13 #Trouble in the Garrison
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Competition Counter
	id = nfa.28
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.28"}
	title = nfa.28.t
	desc = nfa.28.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.28.a
		if = { #Loop Again
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Competition_Loop_Counter
					value = 1
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = Mordacq_Airwaves
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_CSN
					has_country_flag = NATFRA_Democracy_Restored
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
						has_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
					}
				}
				clr_country_flag = nfa_discord_chosen
				NFA_remove_de_gaulle_military_ideas = yes
				clr_country_flag = nfa_no_book_chosen
				set_country_flag = nfa_lessons_1914_chosen
			}
			#Do nothing to end the loop
		}
		else = { #Someone is a Winner
			clr_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			if = { #Check if Mordacq has more influence than Petain
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = Mor_influence
						value = Pet_influence
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				NFA = {
					country_event = { id = nfa.35  days = 7 } # Mordacq coups Petain
					set_country_flag = NFA_Napoleon_0
				}
			}
			else = {
				NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.39  days = 15 } } # Petain has more influence
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Corruption Check
	id = nfa.30
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.30"}
	title = nfa.30.t
	desc = nfa.30.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	hidden = yes

	option = { 
		name = nfa.30.a 
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 6
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf		
			}
			NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.32  days = 1 } } # Corruption still coming
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NFA_event_31
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 5
					compare = less_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = Pet_corruption
					value = 3
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
			}
			NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.31  days = 1 } } # High Corruption warning
			NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.30  days = 7 } } #Loop the checker
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = NFA_Corruption_Checker_cf
				has_country_flag = Fight_for_influence_on
			}
			NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.30  days = 7 } } #Loop the checker
		}
		else = {
			# Nothing to end this loop
		}
	}
}

		PREV = { #Scope to the state that the rails were sabotaged in
			add_state_modifier = { modifier = { disable_strategic_redeployment = -1 } } #A modifier of -1 turns strategic redeployment back on
			add_state_modifier = { modifier = { local_supplies_for_controller = 0.5 } }	#Turn the supplies back to normal
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Divided France GER
	id = nfa.79
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.79"}
	title = nfa.79.t
	desc = nfa.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_weeping

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		always = no #Disable divided France for now, annexations will handle that
		tag = GER
		owns_state = 16
		country_exists = NFA
		21 = {
			OR = {
				is_controlled_by = NFA
				controller = {
					is_subject_of = NFA
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = FRP
			has_country_flag = FRA_CONQ
			NFA = {
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			has_war_with = NFA
			has_global_flag = DEAL_WITH_NFA_ALLY
			has_global_flag = france_refused_bordeaux
			has_country_flag = NFA_refused_land_exchange
			has_country_flag = GER_refused_share_france
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.79.a #Formalise division of France
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		NFA = {
			country_event = {
				id = nfa.80
				days = 1
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = NFA
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = NFA
				modifier = GER_shared_france
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.79.b #No, we refuse such deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_refused_share_france
		add_stability = -0.02

			limit = {
				country_exists = NFA
			}
			reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = NFA
				modifier = GER_refused_share_france
			}
		}
		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = part.6
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.79.c #National France can have that land, if they join us!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = NFA
			NFA = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_subject = yes
					has_war_with = GER
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = DEAL_WITH_NFA_ALLY
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
				country_event = {
					id = part.82
					days = 1
				}
				else = {
					country_event = {
						id = part.81
						days = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_global_flag = DEAL_WITH_NFA_ALLY
	}
}

	}

country_event = { # GER invites us to discuss the occupation of France
	id = nfa.120
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.120" }
	title = nfa.120.t
	desc = nfa.120.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Meet with the Germans
		name = nfa.120.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.05
				has_government = national_populist
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 4
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.134 } } #The French enter negotiations - Case 1
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 3
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.132 } } #The French enter negotiations - Case 2
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 2
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.130 } } #The French enter negotiations - Case 3
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 1
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.128 } } #The French enter negotiations - Case 4
		}

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				count_triggers = {
					amount = 0
					16 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Paris
					19 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Bordeaux
					20 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lyon
					21 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Marseilles
					980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER } #Lille
				}
			}
			GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.125 } } #The French enter negotiations - Case 5
		}

	}

	option = { #Do not fall for the trick
		name = nfa.120.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		GER = { country_event = { id = nfa.121 } } #The French decline talks
	}
}

country_event = { # France declines talks
	id = nfa.121
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.121" }

	desc = nfa.121.d

			factor = 100
		}

			add_ideas = FRP_Arms_Treaty_idea
		}

			limit = {
				980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
				17 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				983 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
				14 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
			}
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # France declines deal
	id = nfa.122

	desc = nfa.122.d

	option = { #Unfortunate
		name = nfa.122.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
		add_manpower = -10000
		GER_release_small_FRP = yes
		FRP = {
			add_ideas = FRP_Arms_Treaty_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_1
					has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_2
				}
			}
			add_ideas = GER_FRP_occupation_cost_2_idea
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GER_FRP_occupation_cost_1_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				980 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
				17 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
			}
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				983 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
				14 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER }
			}
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # France accepts deal
	id = nfa.123
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.123" }
	title = nfa.123.t
	desc = {
		text = nfa.123.d.5 #Peace Deal 5
		trigger = { has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_5 }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.123.d.4 #Peace Deal 4
		trigger = { has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_4 }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.123.d.3 #Peace Deal 3
		trigger = { has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_3 }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.123.d.2 #Peace Deal 2
		trigger = { has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_2 }
	}
	desc = {
		text = nfa.123.d.1 #Peace Deal 1
		trigger = { has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_1 }
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #To a lasting peace!
		name = nfa.123.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_5
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA
			GER_transfer_NFA = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_4
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Greater Belgium
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Belgium = yes
			# Expanded Calais
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_3
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Greater Belgium and Brittany
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Belgium_and_Brittany = yes
			# Expanded Calais
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
			# Make Brittany
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
			# Military Disarmament
			NFA_Military_Accords = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_2
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Greater Belgium and Brittany
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Belgium_and_Brittany = yes
			# Expanded Calais
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
			# Make Brittany
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
			# Military Disarmament
			NFA_Military_Accords_Harsh = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NFA
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = NFA_peace_deal_1
			}
			NFA_Clear_Peace_Deal_Flags = yes
			# Transfer land to NFA except Greater Belgium and Brittany
			GER_transfer_NFA_except_Belgium_and_Brittany = yes
			# Expanded Calais
			NFA_Greater_Belgium_to_GER = yes
			# Make Brittany
			GER_release_Brittany = yes
			# Border Fort Dismantlement
			NFA_Border_Dismantlement = yes
			# Economic Reparations from France
			NFA_Economic_Reparations = yes
			# Military Disarmament
			NFA_Military_Accords_Harsh = yes
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = NFA
				relation = military_access
				active = yes
			}
			set_global_flag = ENT_france_agree_mittel
		}
	}

}

	}

	desc = nfa.153.d

		name = nfa.153.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				country_exists = FRP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				735 = {
					is_controlled_by = SWI # Will say no if they won war against the Communards
				}
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			transfer_state = 943
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SWI
				modifier = NFA_accepted_demands
			}
			remove_state_claim = 943
			add_state_core = 943
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = FRP
			}
			FRP = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = SWI
					modifier = NFA_SWI_disregards_FRP
				}
				add_stability = -0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse to return - FRP exists
		name = nfa.153.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = FRP
		}
		NFA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SWI
				modifier = NFA_ignored_threat
			}
			country_event = nfa.154
		}
	}

	option = { #Refuse to return
		name = nfa.153.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				country_exists = FRP
			}
		}
		NFA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SWI
				modifier = NFA_ignored_threat
			}
			country_event = nfa.154
		}
	}
}

		}

		add_stability = 0.05
		set_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		custom_effect_tooltip = NFA_Algiers_Conference_AF_effect

			# French Saharan Africa #

				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance
					}
				}
				remove_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance
				}
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_target_var
				clear_variable = NFA_colonial_resistance_compliance_var
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = NFA
					is_on_continent = africa
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = NFA
						state = 834 #Gambia
						state = 700 #Sierra Leone
					}
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Autonomous_State }
				force_disable_resistance = NFA
				cancel_resistance = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

			factor = 100
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NFA = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = nfa_transahara_almost_cf
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { temp_255 = random }
				multiply_temp_variable = { temp_255 = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = {
							temp_255 < 86
						}
					}
					NFA = { country_event = { id = nfa.252 days = 75 random = 100 } } # Workers Strike
				}
				else = {
					# Nothing happens
				}
			}
			
		}
		NFA_Longer_Mission_30 = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_decision = Transahara_Phase_One
					has_decision = Transahara_Phase_Two
				}
			}
			513 = {
				damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 0.3 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_decision = Transahara_Phase_Three
					has_decision = Transahara_Phase_Four
				}
			}
			556 = {
				damage_building = { type = infrastructure damage = 0.3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Conclusion of the Purge chain
	id = nfa.317
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.317"}
	title = nfa.317.t
	desc = nfa.317.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = nfa.317.a #A new bonus
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		remove_ideas = NFA_republican_remnants
		set_country_flag = NFA_AF_purge_decisions_over
		if = { #Give the idea of the most clicked option
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_low > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_low_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_medium > NFA_AF_purged_high
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_low
				}
				check_variable = {
					NFA_AF_purged_high > NFA_AF_purged_medium
				}
			}
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_high_idea
		}
		# If there is a tie situation
		else = {
			add_ideas = NFA_AF_purged_medium_idea
		}
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_low
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_medium
		clear_variable = NFA_AF_purged_high
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden event to check if post-war events can fire, depending on owned states and months
	id = nfa.529
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.529"}
	
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 762 #Nice
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.518 days = 8 random = 48 } #Restoration of Monaco
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 21 #Marseille
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.8.29
						date < 1939.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.8.29
						date < 1940.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.8.29
						date < 1941.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.8.29
						date < 1942.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.8.29
						date < 1943.10.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.8.29
						date < 1944.10.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.530 days = 2 } #Festival d'Avignon
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.179 days = 95 } #The question of Montmartre
			country_event = { id = nfa.531 days = 450 } #A mosque in Paris?
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.6.29
						date < 1939.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.6.29
						date < 1940.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.6.29
						date < 1941.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.6.29
						date < 1942.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.6.29
						date < 1943.8.1
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.6.29
						date < 1944.8.1
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.532 days = 2 } #First New Tour de France
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 16 #Paris
				OR = {
					AND = {
						date > 1939.1.29
						date < 1939.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1940.1.29
						date < 1940.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1941.1.29
						date < 1941.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1942.1.29
						date < 1942.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1943.1.29
						date < 1943.2.25
					}
					AND = {
						date > 1944.1.29
						date < 1944.2.25
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.540 days = 2 } #First New Tour de France
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 15 #Normandy
			}
			country_event = { id = nfa.533 days = 160 } #Rouen Reconstruction
			country_event = { id = nfa.534 days = 250 } #Tank in Vimoutiers
		}
		country_event = { id = nfa.529 days = 45 } #Loop the event without jumping over months
	}
}

# French Guinea and Upper Volta

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - French Guinea
	id = nfa.443
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.443"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			806 = { #Guinea
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			808 = { #Upper Volta
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF }
	}

	option = { #Mission Attacked - 444
		trigger = {
			806 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT }
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_guinea_mission_attacked
				806 = { is_core_of = ROOT } #Guinea
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Algeria
	id = nfa.462
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.462"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			owns_state = 16 #Paris
			has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		}
	}

	option = { #Rousing speech from the ENA - 463
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 36
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA
		country_event = nfa.463
		country_event = { id = nfa.462 days = 158 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Street fight between algerian syndies and muslims - 464

			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria }

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.4
				has_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA
				has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.465
		country_event = { id = nfa.462 days = 158 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Nationalist books seized - 466
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.6
				has_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2.6
				has_country_flag = nfa_street_fight_algeria
				has_country_flag = nfa_speech_ENA
			}
		}
		country_event = nfa.466
		country_event = { id = nfa.462 days = 158 random = 96 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens

country_event = { #Hidden event to decide the chain - Senegal
	id = nfa.467
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.467"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			has_country_flag = nfa_resistance_cancelled_algiers_AF
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		country_event = { id = nfa.467 days = 158 random = 36 } #loop
	}

	option = { #Miner strike - 468
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.4
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
		country_event = nfa.468
	}

	option = { #Resentment spreading to Lower classes - 469
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 22
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.14
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
		country_event = nfa.469
	}

	option = { #Evolués support the idea of independence - 470
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 12
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
		country_event = nfa.470
	}

	option = { #Nothing happens
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.08
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.15
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
					has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.42
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.54
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_resentment_lower_class
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_minerstrike
				has_country_flag = nfa_senegal_evolues_independence
			}
		}
	}
}

			515 = { #Chad
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}

			}

# Revolt events from nfa.600

country_event = { #Country released by another revolter
	id = nfa.600
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.600"}
	title = nfa.600.t
	desc = nfa.600.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
			set_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@event_target:revolter
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = event_target:revolter }
				event_target:revolter = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			event_target:original_occupier = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = event_target:revolter
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
			}
			event_target:revolter = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = event_target:original_occupier
					relation = military_access
					active = yes
				}
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						load_oob = [OOB_NAME]
					}
					OOB_NAME = "[revolter.GetTag]_revolt"
				}
				every_controlled_state = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						}
						add_resistance = 7
						add_compliance = -4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.600.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:revolter
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Colony Revolts
	id = nfa.601
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.601"}
	title = nfa.601.t
	desc = nfa.601.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = NFA_active_rebellion
			set_country_flag = NFA_rebelled_@event_target:revolter
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { is_core_of = event_target:revolter }
				event_target:revolter = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			event_target:revolter = {
				meta_effect = {
					text = {
						load_oob = [OOB_NAME]
					}
					OOB_NAME = "[revolter.GetTag]_revolt"
				}
				every_controlled_state = {
					every_neighbor_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
							NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						}
						add_resistance = 15
						add_compliance = -7.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.601.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = event_target:revolter
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = nfa.601.b
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = -150
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_colonial_resistance }
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = NFA_Colonial_Exploitation }
				}
			}
			add_resistance = 15
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Collapse of National France if killed or someone got algeria
	id = nfa.623
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.623" }
	title = nfa.623.t
	desc = nfa.623.d

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		OR = {
			has_capitulated = yes
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 460
				controls_state = 459
				controls_state = 805
				controls_state = 458
			}
		}
		NOT = { #One Major French city is back in our hands
			16 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			19 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			20 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			21 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 4
	}

	option = {
		name = nfa.623.a
		
		### Morocco
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = MOR
				}
				country_exists = MOR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 290 #Rif
						state = 699 #Rio de Oro
					}
				}
				MOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		
		### Kill off NFA
		force_capitulate = yes
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Collapse of National France caused by native revolts with no other invaders
	id = nfa.624
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event nfa.624" }
	title = nfa.624.t
	desc = nfa.624.d

	trigger = {
		tag = NFA
		OR = {
			has_war_with = TUN
			has_war_with = WAD
			has_war_with = NGR
			has_war_with = MAL
			has_war_with = MRT
			has_war_with = BFA
			has_war_with = GNA
			has_war_with = SEN
			has_war_with = SIE
		}
		NOT = {
			any_owned_state = { #You're not being invaded by anyone else than revolters
				controller = {
					NOT = {
						tag = NFA
						tag = TUN
						tag = WAD
						tag = NGR
						tag = MAL
						tag = MRT
						tag = BFA

			20 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
			21 = {
				is_owned_by = NFA
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 513

				controls_state = 805
			}

				controls_state = 459
			}

			NOT = { 
				owns_state = 458 #Literally everything revolted or went to another country
				owns_state = 557

				owns_state = 556

		days = 2

		add_war_support = -0.5

				}
			}
		}

				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUN
				}
				TUN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		### Mauritania
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MRT
			}
			MRT = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
